  var isDebugPage = window.location.href.match(/\/debug\/set-speedtrap\/index.html$/);
  var isPreviewPage = window.location.hostname.search(/^.*preview.*$/) !== -1;
  if (isDebugPage || isPreviewPage) return;

  var screenWidth = window.innerWidth;
  var viewportTooLarge = screenWidth >= data.width;

  var getCookieValue = function getCookieValue(name) {
    var matches = document.cookie.match(new RegExp("(^|;)\\s*".concat(name, "\\s*=\\s*([^;]+)")));

    if (matches) {
      return matches.pop();
    }

    return null;
  };

  var noCookieOrExceedsThreshold = !cookieValue || parseInt(cookieValue, 10) >= data.cookie.redirCutoffValue;
  var dtCookieValue = getCookieValue(data.dtCookie.name);
  var dtNoCookieOrExceedsThreshold = !dtCookieValue || parseInt(dtCookieValue, 10) >= data.dtCookie.redirCutoffValue;

  var findMatch = function findMatch(hosts) {
    return hosts.find(function (_ref) {
      var host = _ref.host;
      return window.location.hostname === host;
    });
  };

  var redirReplace = function redirReplace(redirBlockParam) {
    var match = findMatch(data.hosts);

    if (match && match.dest) {
      return window.location.replace("//".concat(match.dest).concat(window.location.pathname, "?").concat(redirBlockParam, "=").concat(Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000)));
    }

    return null;
  };

  if (viewportTooLarge) {
    // if in a larger viewport, check to see if user has the desktop/tablet cookie. if not, redirect them to michonne
    if (dtNoCookieOrExceedsThreshold) {
      var redirBlockParam = data.dtCookie.redirBlockParam;
      redirReplace(redirBlockParam);
    } // if in a smaller viewport, check to see if user has the mobile cookie. if not, redirect them to michonne

  } else if (!serviceWorkersSupported || noCookieOrExceedsThreshold) {
    var _redirBlockParam = data.cookie.redirBlockParam;
    redirReplace(_redirBlockParam);
  }

_9db439e9 speakable"><b data-type="sourceText">Washington <!-- -->(CNN)<!-- --> <!-- --> </b><span>Michael Cohen's <a href="/2018/11/29/politics/michael-cohen-guilty-plea-misleading-congress/index.html" target="_blank">admission that he lied to Congress</a> about Donald Trump's knowledge of the ongoing effort to build a Trump Tower in Moscow during the 2016 campaign has ensnared the President's children in special counsel Robert Mueller's investigation. </span></div><div class="b5d1cb4d _9db439e9"><a aria-label="Related Article: Michael Cohen pleads guilty, says he lied about Trump's knowledge of Moscow project" aria-disabled="false" class="_0308207a " href="/2018/11/29/politics/michael-cohen-guilty-plea-misleading-congress/index.html" name="Related Article: Michael Cohen pleads guilty, says he lied about Trump's knowledge of Moscow project" icon="" target=""><div><div class="_2a5c0c94"><div class="dbee38e0"></div></div></div></a><div class="_49fb7f0e cnnds_txt_grey_small"><a aria-label="Related Article: Michael Cohen pleads guilty, says he lied about Trump's knowledge of Moscow project" aria-disabled="false" class="_0308207a _1e227843 " href="/2018/11/29/politics/michael-cohen-guilty-plea-misleading-congress/index.html" name="Related Article: Michael Cohen pleads guilty, says he lied about Trump's knowledge of Moscow project" icon="" target=""><span><b>Related Article:</b> Michael Cohen pleads guilty, says he lied about Trump's knowledge of Moscow project</span></a></div></div><div class="body-text_BodyText__UjdHO _9db439e9 speakable">After previously saying that the Moscow project had stopped in January 2016, just before the Iowa caucuses, Cohen said Thursday in federal court that discussions actually continued until June 2016 -- when Trump was the presumptive Republican nominee. </div><div class="_53039000"><div id="ad_rect_atf_02" class="ad-ad_rect_atf_02 _146ce769 _18afb79b"></div></div><div class="body-text_BodyText__UjdHO _9db439e9 speakable">Cohen, in accepting a plea deal, admitted that he had "more extensive communications" than the three he previously indicated he had with Trump, which he previously claimed lasted no more than a few minutes, and added that he "briefed" Trump family members about the project. The guilty plea doesn't state which family members Cohen is referring to or when he spoke with them. It would not be illegal to discuss the plans with Trump's children, who were helping steer the business. </div><div class="body-text_BodyText__UjdHO _9db439e9">At least one of Trump's children, Donald Trump Jr., a loyal surrogate for his father on the campaign trail, has provided testimony under oath to at least three congressional committees where he was asked about the proposed deal. Most of that testimony is not public and it isn't clear how detailed the questions were about the project. Yet it could place him in legal jeopardy if anything he told Congress conflicts with information provided by Cohen if it is supported by other evidence. </div><div class="body-text_BodyText__UjdHO _9db439e9">A person close to the company tells CNN that Trump Jr. did know about the project as did his sister, Ivanka, whose involvement was limited to recommending architects and designers. The source says Trump Jr.'s testimony that his knowledge was "peripheral" is "100% accurate." </div><div class="read-more-button"><div class="_53039000 e2048ec6"><button aria-label="" class="_1acd87bf" aria-disabled="false" href="" target="" type="">Read more</button></div></div><div class="componentHidden"><div class="footer-note_FooterNote__23Z7a fa2329bc"><hr><p class="cnnds_txt_grey_small">CNN's Liz Stark, Katelyn Polantz and Marshall Cohen contributed to this report.</p></div></div></div><div><div class="_53039000"><div class="c93b5e1d"><div class="OUTBRAIN" data-src="edition.cnn.com/2018/11/29/politics/donald-trump-jr-cohen-trump-organization/index.html" data-widget-id="MB_13" data-ob-template="cnn"></div></div></div><div class="_53039000"></div><div class="_53039000"></div></div><div></div><div></div></div></div><div class="_53039000"><div class="PartnerZone"><div></div></div><div id="ad_bnr_btf_01" class="ad-ad_bnr_btf_01 _146ce769 _18afb79b"></div></div></div></div><div id="ad_nat_btf_01" class="ad-ad_nat_btf_01 _146ce769 _18afb79b _3b5323b0 _0e65240c"></div><div><div></div></div></div><noscript>&lt;p&gt;Please enable JavaScript for a better experience.&lt;/p&gt;</noscript><script type="text/javascript" src="/js/manifest_066517bb.js"></script><script type="text/javascript" src="/js/vendor_066517bb.js"></script><iframe src="https://a125375509.cdn.optimizely.com/client_storage/a125375509.html" hidden="" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" height="0" width="0" style="display: none;"></iframe><script type="text/javascript" src="/js/main_066517bb.js"></script><script src="//registry.api.cnn.io/bundles/fave/2.13.1/js" id="script-FAVE" async="" defer=""></script><script src="//cdn.cnn.com/analytics/cnnexpan/jsmd.min.js" id="script-JSMD" async="" defer=""></script></body></html>
